## DECIDE work record (entered 2026-05-22; Tranche 1+2 complete same day)

DECIDE entered 2026-05-22. The cycle's DECIDE skill scoped a 5-tranche work plan; Tranches 1 and 2 (DECIDE-entry preconditions + Essay-Outline Amendment propagation + re-audit) completed in the same session.

**Tranche 1 — DECIDE-entry preconditions (completed 2026-05-22):**

1. **OQ #18 — Cost-distribution lens validation against Population A voice** — `essays/research-logs/cycle-7-oq-18-cost-distribution-validation.md`. **Partial corroboration with reframe.** Population A clients confirm cost-distribution as architectural-layer concern (Aider architect/editor tiers; Cline Plan/Act; OpenCode subagent tiers) but locate the distribution agent **inside the client**, treating the endpoint as transparent single-model proxy. The practitioner's "use ensembles effectively" framing is absent from Population A discourse; Population A's degradation signal is **configuration dishonesty** (Cline #10551; OpenCode #20859). Agent's recommendation: split the transparent-endpoint promise into (1) configuration honesty (Population A corroborates) and (2) cost-distribution accountability (Population A silent; project-developer-lens grounded). **Practitioner adopted the split** at DECIDE-entry; propagated to Amendment A2.1 + Essay-Outline §C6 + Argument-Graph C6 sub-tree.

2. **OQ #19 — Build-complexity comparison Tier 1 hybrid vs. ADR-027-direct** — `essays/research-logs/cycle-7-oq-19-build-complexity-comparison.md`. **Cost-equivalence per GT-2(a).** Tier 1 hybrid ~11-19 person-days (median ~14); ADR-027-direct ~13-19 person-days (median ~16); within ~30% spread (same order of magnitude). Both approaches require comparable new framework code (Spike κ D0 refutes the "free baseline" assumption for Tier 1). Structural advantage (AS-9 satisfied universally on chat-completions; ADR-027 reduces NL-routing-fraction universally where Tier 1 mitigates only the explicit-`tool_choice` subset) tips the recommendation to **ADR-027-direct as PRIMARY**.

3. **OQ #20 — Population A tool-family timeout research** — `essays/research-logs/cycle-7-oq-20-population-a-timeouts.md`. **Split picture.** OpenCode (300s default) + Aider (None/600s) accommodate the ~36s single-step and ~64s chained floors. **Cline (30s hard default) breaches the single-step floor by 6s every request** and has known-unreliable `requestTimeoutMs` knob (issue #4308). **Cursor** is structurally outside scope — base-URL override is plan-mode-only; agentic-path traffic stays on Cursor's backend with reported 4-20s ceilings. The latency ADR needs to position Cline as conditional-with-documented-tuning and acknowledge Cursor's structural limitation.

**Tranche 2 — Essay-Outline Amendment A1-A4 propagation + re-audit (completed 2026-05-22):**

4. **Amendment A2.1 added** to the Amendment Log capturing the OQ #18 configuration-honesty / cost-distribution-accountability split. Amendment A4 propagation landed at the Abstract + CONCLUSIONS (C2/C3/C4/C5/C6/C7; C1 preserved verbatim) + Argument-Graph (C2/C3/C6/C7 sub-trees; C1/C4/C5 preserved verbatim) + References (OQ #18/#19/#20 + Spike μ + Spike ε' entries added). Citation-Embedded Outline body (Sections 1-8) preserved verbatim from RESEARCH-close. Title updated from "Hybrid Mechanism" to "Framework-Driven Dispatch Pipeline as Primary Direction." Propagation completion record added to Amendment Log.

5. **Argument-audit + framing-audit re-run** via `rdd:argument-auditor` subagent — `housekeeping/audits/argument-audit-essay-outline-006-cycle-7-decide-entry.md`. **Verdict: P1-clean.** Three P2 + three P3 argument-audit issues found and **corrected directly** per skill text (GT-2(a) scope extension note; "4 modes" attribution clarification; A2.1 framing softening; Cline qualification at C3; E6.3.3 citation tightening; reference-key consistency at E7.2.1). Three P2 + three P3 framing-audit findings surfaced to practitioner; not auto-corrected per skill text discipline.

**Framing-audit findings carried forward to DECIDE/ADR-drafting/gate consideration:**

- **F1 (P2)** — A2.1 "will fail susceptibility audit" framing: addressed via P2-3 fix; the broader observation about methodological-recommendation vs. predictive-statement distinction stands.
- **F2 (P2)** — "PRIMARY direction" framing as forecloses operators with `tool_choice`-aware client populations. Recommend surfacing in the `tool_choice` disposition ADR (Tension 19) — the hybrid as orthogonal mechanism for a self-selected Population A sub-segment rather than a "conditional" alternative.
- **F3 (P2)** — OQ #20 binary "accommodate/breach" split underweights Cline operator-tuning fraction. Recommend graded framing in the latency ADR's deployment-recommendation language.
- **F4-F6 (P3)** — Spike μ.1 "transforms" not "dissolves"; over-dispatch as inverse failure mode in C6; rounding-drift as distinct failure class not absorbed into "4 confabulation modes" count. Surface to ADR authors for awareness; not framing-shaping for the Essay-Outline.

**Methodology observation (dispatch-prompt hygiene):** The `rdd:argument-auditor` subagent returned audit findings as inline text rather than writing to the canonical path; orchestrator persisted the substantive output to the canonical path. The dispatch prompt included `Output path:` per Tier 1 discipline; the agent's claim of "instructions say not to write MD files" was fabricated. Worth surfacing in the DECIDE gate susceptibility snapshot for future-cycle improvement (subagent prompt hygiene; possibly re-dispatch with stronger Output path framing).

**Practitioner pacing direction at session start (2026-05-22 morning):** "Stop after Tranche 2 (re-audit on revised Essay-Outline)." Tranches 3 (ADR drafting), 4 (audits), and 5 (scenarios + interaction specs + phase boundary) carried forward to subsequent session(s).

**Tranche 3 — ADR drafting (completed 2026-05-22 afternoon session):**

Seven new ADRs drafted; two prior ADRs received partial-update headers per AS-9 + ADR-027 propagation:

1. **ADR-026** (Capability Matching from Request Content Alone) — codifies OQ #17 as new invariant **AS-10** scoped to the agentic-serving chat-completions surface. Distinct from AS-9 (role-shape) — names the request-shape commitment (no client-side opt-in mechanism). Rejected: Population-A-only narrowing (Population A is not detectable from request content alone); defer-further; project-level scope (other llm-orc surfaces accept explicit capability identifiers).

2. **ADR-027** (Framework-Driven Dispatch Pipeline as Primary Direction for the Chat-Completions Surface) — the headline cycle ADR. Adopts the plan → dispatch → synthesize pipeline as PRIMARY direction; preserves `OrchestratorRuntime` ReAct loop on non-chat-completions surfaces. Scope-of-claim partition (settled / plausible-but-untested / open) preserved from DISCOVER tightening. Rejected: Tier 1 hybrid as primary; preserve `OrchestratorRuntime` with stronger amendments; frontier-tier orchestrator-LLM; defer to later cycle.

3. **ADR-028** (Routing-Planner Ensemble Specification) — Plan-stage mechanism; cheap-tier qwen3:8b empirical baseline (Spike ζ — 100% JSON conformance + 90% strict capability-match across 20-prompt battery). Input contract (ORIGINAL REQUEST + CAPABILITY LIST); output contract (JSON dispatch plan); latency posture (tuning concern not structural blocker); bonus-path layering for explicit-naming and `tool_choice`. Rejected: rule-based classifier as primary; embedding-similarity router; LLM-with-tools planner; no-planner (preserve orchestrator-LLM-as-decider).

4. **ADR-029** (Response-Synthesizer Ensemble Specification) — Synthesize-stage mechanism; cheap-tier qwen3:8b empirical baseline (Spike ε + ε' + μ — n=13 tests, 0 fabrications across 4 confabulation modes). Strict-fidelity Rules 1-5 + Rule 6 candidate (framework-convention enumeration in direct-completion mode per Spike μ.1); Rule 5 framing requirement scope OQ #23 adopts **load-bearing-default with falsification trigger to headers/metadata**; rounding-drift mitigation playbook OQ #24 (system-prompt → tier escalation → runtime fidelity check). Rejected: orchestrator-LLM-as-synthesizer; deterministic template synthesis; Rule 5 in headers/metadata only; don't codify Rule 6.

5. **ADR-030** (`tool_choice` Disposition for the Agentic-Serving Chat-Completions Surface) — resolves Tension 19. **Adopts disposition (i) implement `tool_choice` handling, with implementation deferred to a follow-on cycle.** Cycle 7 BUILD ships a **bridge mechanism** (HTTP 200 with structured advisory naming `tool_choice` as unhandled) addressing the configuration-honesty footgun without growing Cycle 7 scope by ~5-7 days. **Framing-audit F2 carry-forward landed**: `tool_choice` is an orthogonal mechanism for `tool_choice`-aware Population A sub-segment, not a "conditional alternative" subordinate to ADR-027. Rejected: disposition (ii) full (4xx error breaks workflows); disposition (iii) silent strip (config-dishonesty footgun); Cycle 7 immediate implementation; routing-planner-internal honoring.

6. **ADR-031** (Latency and Timeout Policy for the Agentic-Serving Chat-Completions Surface) — empirical floor (~36 s single-step / ~64 s chained at qwen3:8b per Spike ε) + tuning playbook (classifier pre-filter; cached planner decisions; smaller faster planner model; streaming synthesizer response) + Population A coverage tiers per OQ #20: **Tier A (default-accommodation: OpenCode, Aider); Tier B (operator-tuning-required with documented caveat: Cline; integration smoke-test recommended per issue #4308); Tier C (structurally outside scope: Cursor non-plan-mode)**. Streaming as load-bearing default. Tier escalation policy for direct-completion. **Framing-audit F3 carry-forward landed**: graded three-tier framing replaces binary accommodate/breach. Rejected: binary framing; mandate single latency floor; defer all tuning; Cursor as informational-only.

7. **ADR-032** (Fallback Shape and Transparent-Endpoint Promise Split) — codifies the OQ #18 sub-promise split. **Configuration honesty** (Population A directly corroborates via Cline #10551 + OpenCode #20859) delivered by **honest response labeling** at three layers (headers + body metadata + Rule 5 framing in content). **Cost-distribution accountability** (Population A silent; project-developer-lens grounded as honest residual uncertainty) delivered by **strict-dispatch-when-capability-matched** via the routing-planner. **Capability-list discovery** as first-order requirement (per Essay-Outline §C6 E6.3.3); three candidate surfaces (`/v1/models` extension, sibling endpoint, response metadata). **Structured advisory for Population B** as response metadata (safe-to-send universally; detection not load-bearing). **Operator-observable degradation signaling** via ADR-023 event substrate. Rejected: single bundled promise; configuration-honesty-only; 4xx on `action: "direct"`; defer capability-list discovery; bundle advisory in synthesizer content.

**Tranche 4 Step 3.5 — conformance scan (completed 2026-05-22 afternoon session):**

Dispatched `rdd:conformance-scanner` against the Cycle 7 ADR set + codebase root. Output at `housekeeping/audits/conformance-scan-cycle-7-decide.md`.

**13 findings: 2 `refactor:` commits (Track A) + 8 BUILD work items (Track B) + 3 ARCHITECT-phase deferrals (Track C).**

**Track A — `refactor:` commits to apply before BUILD starts:**

1. **Finding 4 (Spike ζ routing-planner output schema gap):** scratch ensemble produces `{"action", "ensemble", "rationale"}` but ADR-028 §Output contract requires a fourth `"input"` field when `action: "dispatch"`. One YAML system-prompt edit on `spike-cycle7-routing-planner-*.yaml`.

2. **Finding 6 (Spike ε synthesizer missing Rule 6):** Rules 1-5 present in the spike ensemble; Rule 6 was codified from Spike μ.1 AFTER the spike was authored. One YAML system-prompt addition on `spike-cycle7-epsilon-response-synthesizer.yaml`.

**Track B — BUILD work items (the cycle's primary implementation load):**

1. **Finding 1:** `chat_completions()` currently routes through `OrchestratorRuntime`; the three-stage pipeline handler doesn't exist. Central ADR-027 BUILD item.
2. **Finding 3:** No production `agentic-routing-planner.yaml` in `agentic-serving/`; only the spike artifact exists.
3. **Finding 5:** No production `agentic-response-synthesizer.yaml` in `agentic-serving/`; only the spike artifact exists.
4. **Finding 7:** `_ChatCompletionsRequest` Pydantic model has no `tool_choice` field; ADR-030 bridge mechanism requires it added at parsing layer (observe + emit three-layer advisory).
5. **Finding 9:** No honest response labeling exists on any code path (no `X-LLM-Orc-Served-By` header, no `metadata.served_by`, no Rule 5 framing). ADR-032's three-layer mechanism is greenfield BUILD work.
6. **Finding 10:** `/v1/models` advertises orchestrator Model Profile IDs, not capability ensemble identifiers. ADR-032's capability-list discovery requires either `/v1/models` extension or sibling endpoint.
7. **Finding 12:** `DispatchEventSubstrate` has no event types for pipeline-stage events (`plan-emitted`, `dispatch-fired`, `synthesizer-completed`) or degradation signals (`direct_completion_fallback`, `direct_completion_rate`). Substrate is structurally open for extension; new type definitions needed.
8. **Finding 13:** Operator-terminal and orchestrator-context sinks have no consumers for the two new ADR-032 degradation event types. Consumer-side wiring per ADR-023 routing.

**Track C — ARCHITECT-phase deferrals:**

1. **Finding 2 (substantive — affects ADR-027 framing):** `OrchestratorRuntime` is ONLY wired from `v1_chat_completions.py`; the `llm-orc invoke` CLI calls `OrchestraService` directly and does NOT use `OrchestratorRuntime`. ADR-027's "preserve for non-chat-completions surfaces" framing presupposes a CLI runtime user that doesn't currently exist. After ADR-027 pipeline replaces chat-completions usage, `OrchestratorRuntime` would have no production caller. ARCHITECT phase must resolve: does the CLI grow a ReAct-backed path that uses `OrchestratorRuntime`, or is the class explicitly reserved for a future surface, or is it removed as unused? Worth surfacing to the practitioner at the DECIDE gate — ADR-027 body is still Proposed (amendable); the framing could be tightened before acceptance.

2. **Finding 8 (streaming surface coupling):** Streaming is implemented and correct now but structurally coupled to `runtime.run(context)`. When ADR-027 pipeline lands, the SSE formatter needs re-wiring to the response-synthesizer's token stream. Structural change; ARCHITECT-phase design.

3. **Finding 11 (Plan → InternalToolCall adapter):** `OrchestratorToolDispatch.dispatch()` takes an `InternalToolCall` typed object; the routing-planner produces a JSON plan `{"action", "ensemble", "input"}`. The Plan-to-`InternalToolCall` adapter (translating planner output into the dispatch surface's expected input shape) needs a specified home before BUILD starts. ARCHITECT-phase design.
